\ifproblemToFind% If it has a desirable problem search the file.
%%\tagged{Ans@MC, Type@Concept, Topic@Integral, Sub@Definite, Sub@Theorems-FTC, Func@Rational, File@0001}{
\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Integration Concept Question 0001. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

What is wrong with the following equation:

\[
\int_{-5}^{4} {\frac{3}{x}}\;dx = {3 \, \log\left(x\right)}\Bigg\vert_{-5}^{4} = {-3 i \, \pi - 3 \, \log\left(5\right) + 3 \, \log\left(4\right)}
\]

\input{Integral-Concept-0001.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{The bounds are evaluated in the wrong order.}
\choice{The antiderivative is incorrect.}
\choice[correct]{The integrand is not defined over the entire interval.}
\choice{Nothing is wrong.  The equation is correct, as is.}
\end{multipleChoice}

\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Integration Concept Question 0001. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{The bounds are evaluated in the wrong order.}
\choice{The antiderivative is incorrect.}
\choice[correct]{The integrand is not defined over the entire interval.}
\choice{Nothing is wrong.  The equation is correct, as is.}
\end{multipleChoice}

\end{problem}}%}

\int_{-5}^{5} {-\frac{8}{x^{3}}}\;dx = {\frac{4}{x^{2}}}\Bigg\vert_{-5}^{5} = {0}
\]

\input{Integral-Concept-0001.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{The bounds are evaluated in the wrong order.}
\choice{The antiderivative is incorrect.}
\choice[correct]{The integrand is not defined over the entire interval.}
\choice{Nothing is wrong.  The equation is correct, as is.}
\end{multipleChoice}

\end{problem}}%}

\int_{-5}^{1} {\frac{4}{x^{2}}}\;dx = {-\frac{4}{x}}\Bigg\vert_{-5}^{1} = {-\frac{24}{5}}
\]

\input{Integral-Concept-0001.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{The bounds are evaluated in the wrong order.}
\choice{The antiderivative is incorrect.}
\choice[correct]{The integrand is not defined over the entire interval.}
\choice{Nothing is wrong.  The equation is correct, as is.}
\end{multipleChoice}

\end{problem}}%}

\int_{-4}^{5} {\frac{7}{x^{2}}}\;dx = {-\frac{7}{x}}\Bigg\vert_{-4}^{5} = {-\frac{63}{20}}
\]

\input{Integral-Concept-0001.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{The bounds are evaluated in the wrong order.}
\choice{The antiderivative is incorrect.}
\choice[correct]{The integrand is not defined over the entire interval.}
\choice{Nothing is wrong.  The equation is correct, as is.}
\end{multipleChoice}

\end{problem}}%}

\int_{-4}^{5} {-\frac{1}{x^{3}}}\;dx = {\frac{1}{2 \, x^{2}}}\Bigg\vert_{-4}^{5} = {-\frac{9}{800}}
\]

\input{Integral-Concept-0001.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{The bounds are evaluated in the wrong order.}
\choice{The antiderivative is incorrect.}
\choice[correct]{The integrand is not defined over the entire interval.}
\choice{Nothing is wrong.  The equation is correct, as is.}
\end{multipleChoice}

\end{problem}}%}

\choice{The bounds are evaluated in the wrong order.}
\choice{The antiderivative is incorrect.}
\choice[correct]{The integrand is not defined over the entire interval.}
\choice{Nothing is wrong.  The equation is correct, as is.}
\end{multipleChoice}

\end{problem}}%}
